        $(document).ready(function () {

            // show thge logo on scroll
            $(document).bind('scroll', function () {
                if ($(this).scrollTop() > 225) {
                    $("#smalllogo").fadeIn('1000');
                    $("#profilebar").addClass("scrolled");
                } else {
                    $("#smalllogo").hide();
                    $("#profilebar").removeClass("scrolled");
                }
            });
            $("#searchinput").autocomplete({
                source: "autocomplete.php",
                minLength: 3,
                select: function (event, ui) {
                    var url = ui.item.id;
                    if (url != '#') {
                        location.href = '/' + url;
                    }
                },
                open: function (event, ui) {
                    $(".ui-autocomplete").css("z-index", 1000);
                }
            });


            $("#banner").click(
                function (e) {
                    if (e.target.id == "banner") {
                        window.location = 'https://www.crossresults.com';
                    }
                }
            );
            $("#searchinput").click(
                function () { return false; }
            );

            $("#searchform").submit(function () {
                return $("#searchinput").val() != "";
            });

        });

        if (!document.addEventListener) {
            //IE8 fix
            $(function () {
                //DOM has loaded, put your code here
                setupResponsiveNav();
            });
        }
        else {
            document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () { setupResponsiveNav(); })
        }


        function setupResponsiveNav() {
            $("#nav").show();

            /* call responsive nav */
            var navigation = responsiveNav("#nav", { // Selector: The ID of the wrapper
                animate: true, // Boolean: Use CSS3 transitions, true or false
                transition: 400, // Integer: Speed of the transition, in milliseconds
                label: "menu", // String: Label for the navigation toggle
                insert: "before", // String: Insert the toggle before or after the navigation
                customToggle: "", // Selector: Specify the ID of a custom toggle
                openPos: "relative", // String: Position of the opened nav, relative or static
                jsClass: "js", // String: 'JS enabled' class which is added to <html> el
                init: function () { }, // Function: Init callback
                open: function () { }, // Function: Open callback
                close: function () { } // Function: Close callback
            });
        }
        function UpdateUpgrades() {
            var cat = $("#category").val();
            var region = $("#region").val();

            $.cookie("upgradecategory", cat, { expires: 30 });
            $.cookie("upgraderegion", region, { expires: 30 });

            var ajaxMsg = "<div style=\"text-align:center;\"><img src=\"img/snake_transparent.gif\"/></div>";
            $("#upgradeboard").html(ajaxMsg);

            $("#upgradeboard").load("upgradeboard.php?cat=" + cat + "&region=" + region + "&sn=r");
        }

$(document).ready(function(){ 
	
    $(".getRacersButton").click(function() {
        var searchText = $("#searchText").val();
		if(searchText.length > 0)
		{
			var url = "ajaxracers.php?s="+escape(searchText) + "&team=yes&confirm=1";
			
			$(".target").html("<img src='img/snake_transparent.gif'/>");
			$(".target").load(url, function(response, status, xhr){			
				});
			$(".input").hide();
			$("#profilesearchresults").show();
		}
		else
		{
			alert('Type your name in the box first, guy');
			$("#searchText").val('THIS BOX!');
			$("#searchText").focus();
			$("#searchText").select();
		}
        });
	$(".togglelogin").click(function(){
		$("#loginform").modal({maxWidth: 600,overlayClose:true, maxHeight: 600 });
		$("#CreateAccountButton").click(function(){
            
            var email = $("#newemail").val();
            var pass = $("#newpass").val();
            var racerID = $("#racerID").val();
            var valid = true;
            var error = "";
            if(email.indexOf("@") == -1)
            {
                valid = false;
                error = "Invalid email.";
            }
            if(pass.length == 0)
            {
                valid = false;
                error = "No zero length passwords.";
            }
            if(valid)
            {
                          
				
                var data = { email: email, pass: pass, racerID:racerID };
                $("#CreateAccountTarget").html("<div style=\"text-align: center\">Creating Account...</div>");                
                $("#CreateAccountTarget").load("procNewAccount.php",data);
            }
            else
            {
                alert(error);
            }
            return false;
        });
		return false;
	});
	$("#SubmitButton").click(function(){
            //var pass = $("#newpass").val();
            //var hexpass = hex_md5(pass);  
            //$("#newpass").val(hexpass);
        });
    $("#regiononly").click(function(){
        var checked = ($("#regiononly").is(':checked'));
        window.location = "setprofile.php?setregionpref="+checked;
    });
    $("a.togglebutton").click(function(){
			
            $(this).next().toggle("slow");
            var expander = $(this).children().children("img");
            if(expander.attr("src") == "img/minus.png")
            {
                expander.attr("src","img/plus.png");
            }
            else
            {
                expander.attr("src","img/minus.png");
            }
            return false;
        });
	    
});

}

                        <script type="text/javascript">

	function FilterByPointsCategory(table,pointscategory)
	{
		var counter = 1;
		table.find("tr").each(function(){ 
			
			if(!$(this).hasClass("headerrow3"))
			{
				var rowPointsCategory = $(this).attr("data-points-category");
				var showRow = rowPointsCategory == pointscategory || pointscategory==""; 
				if(showRow){
					$(this).show();
					$(this).find(":first").children("span").text(counter);
					counter++;
				} else {
					$(this).hide();
				}
			}
		});
	}
	function FilterByAgeAndCategory(table)
	{
		var minAge = 1;
		var maxAge = 100;

		var minCat = table.closest(".racecategory").attr("min-cat");
		var maxCat = table.closest(".racecategory").attr("max-cat");
		var age = table.closest(".racecategory").attr("age-selection");

		if(!age) {
			age = "All";
		}
		if(age != "All") {
			if(age == "U20") maxAge = 19;
			else if(age == "60+") minAge = 60;
			else
			{
				var tokens = age.split("-");
				minAge = parseInt(tokens[0]);
				maxAge = parseInt(tokens[1]);
			}
		}
		
		var counter = 1;

		if(age != "All" || minCat != 1 || maxCat != 5) {
			table.find(".filterdesc").show();
		} else {
			table.find(".filterdesc").hide();
		}
		
		table.find("tr").each(function(){ 
			
			if(!$(this).hasClass("headerrow3"))
			{
				var rowAge = $(this).attr("data-age");
				var rowCat = $(this).attr("cat");
				if(rowCat == "?")
					rowCat = 5;

									rowAge = parseInt(rowAge);
					rowAge = rowAge+1;
								
				var showRow = ((rowAge >= minAge && rowAge <= maxAge) || age == "All") && ( (rowCat >= minCat && rowCat <= maxCat) || (minCat ==1 && maxCat == 5));
				if(showRow){
					$(this).show();
					$(this).find(":first").children("span").text(counter);
					counter++;
				} else {
					$(this).hide();
				}
			}
		});
	}
	
	function doPopup(title)
	{
		$(".popup").modal({overlayClose:true});		
	}  
    var scrollTo = function(_targetObj) {
   
        console.log(typeof $(_targetObj), _targetObj);
  
        if ($(_targetObj).length == 0) {
            return false;
        }

        var body = $("html, body");
  
        var augmentScrollBy = $('.utility').outerHeight() + 10;
        console.log('scrolling');
  
        body.animate({
            scrollTop:$(_targetObj).offset().top - augmentScrollBy}, '500', function() { /* console.log('scroll complete'); */ 
        });
    }
    $(document).ready(function(){   
        $(".download").click(function(){ $(this).hide(); $(this).next().fadeToggle() });
        if (window.location.hash.length) {
            scrollTo(window.location.hash);
          }
          $('a[href^=#]').on('click',function(e){
            e.preventDefault();
            scrollTo($(this).attr('href'));
            window.location.hash = $(this).attr('href');
          });
    
        $("#clearstuff").click(function(){
            $("select").val("");
        });

            var url = document.getElementById("photoinput").value;
            var ajaxurl = "ajaxphoto.php?raceID=12049&add="+escape(url);
           if(url.indexOf(".") > 0)
				$("#ajaxtarget").load(ajaxurl);
			else
				alert("'" + url + "' doesn't look like a valid url to me!");
            });

        $(".togglepoints").click(function(){
			var raceCatId = $(this).attr("CatID");
			if($(this).text() == "Show Points")
			{
				$(this).text("Hide Points");
			}
			else
			{
				$(this).text("Show Points");
			}
            TogglePoints(raceCatId);
            return false;
            });
        $(".togglecats").click(function(){
			var raceCatId = $(this).attr("CatID");
			if($(this).text() == "Show Categories")
			{
				$(this).text("Hide Categories");
			}
			else
			{
				$(this).text("Show Categories");
			}
            ToggleCats(raceCatId);
            return false;
            });

			FilterByPointsCategory($(this).closest(".racecategory").find("table.resultstable"),filter);
		});
		$(".filter").click(function(){
			var minAge = $(this).attr("min-age");
			var maxAge = $(this).attr("max-age");
			var minCat = $(this).attr("min-cat");
			var maxCat = $(this).attr("max-cat");

			if(minAge == 0) minAge = 1;
			if(maxAge == 0) maxAge = 100;
			if(minCat == 0) minCat = 1;
			if(maxCat == 0) maxCat = 5;

			var ageSelection = minAge + "-"+ maxAge;
			$(this).closest(".racecategory").attr("age-selection",ageSelection);
			$(this).closest(".racecategory").attr("min-cat",minCat);
			$(this).closest(".racecategory").attr("max-cat",maxCat);
			$(this).closest(".racecategory").find(".ageselector .minAge").val(minAge);
			$(this).closest(".racecategory").find(".ageselector .maxAge").val(maxAge);
			$(this).closest(".racecategory").find(".categoryselector .minCat").val(minCat);
			$(this).closest(".racecategory").find(".categoryselector .maxCat").val(maxCat);

			FilterByAgeAndCategory($(this).closest(".racecategory").find("table.resultstable"))

			if(ageSelection != "1-100"){
				$(this).closest(".racecategory").find(".ageselector .custom-inputs").fadeIn();
			}
			if(minCat != 1 || maxCat != 5){
				$(this).closest(".racecategory").find(".categoryselector .custom-inputs").fadeIn();
			}
		});
		$(".add-filter").click(function(){ $(this).next().fadeToggle();});
		$(".categoryselector .all").click(function(){
			$(this).closest(".racecategory").attr("min-cat",1);
			$(this).closest(".racecategory").attr("max-cat",5);
			var ageSelection = $(this).closest(".racecategory").attr("age-selection");
			if(!ageSelection) {
				$(this).closest(".racecategory").attr("age-selection","All");
			}
			$(this).closest(".racecategory").find(".minCat").val(1);
			$(this).closest(".racecategory").find(".maxCat").val(5);


			FilterByAgeAndCategory($(this).closest(".racecategory").find("table.resultstable"));
			var me = $(this);


			$(this).parent().children(".categoryselector a").each(function(){
				if(! $(this).is(me)){
					$(this).css("font-weight","normal");
				} else {
					$(this).css("font-weight","bold");
				}
			});
		});
		$(".minAge, .maxAge").keyup(function(){
			var minAge = $(this).parent().children(".minAge").val();
			var maxAge = $(this).parent().children(".maxAge").val();
			ageSelection = minAge + "-" + maxAge;

			$(this).closest(".racecategory").attr("age-selection",ageSelection);

		 $(".ageselector a").click(function(){ 
		 
			var age = $(this).text();			
			var me =  $(this);
			
			//unselect peers
			$(this).parent().children(".ageselector a").each(function(){
				if(! $(this).is(me)){
					if($(this).hasClass("custom") && me.hasClass("ageselected")) {
						$(this).next().toggle();
					}
				
					$(this).css("font-weight","normal");
					me.removeClass("ageselected")
				}
			});			
			if(!me.hasClass("ageselected")){
				me.css("font-weight","bold");
				me.addClass("ageselected")
				if(age != "Custom") {
					
					$(this).closest(".racecategory").attr("age-selection",age);
					FilterByAgeAndCategory($(this).closest(".racecategory").find("table.resultstable"));
				} else {
					$(this).next().toggle();
				}
				
			} else {
				me.css("font-weight","normal");
				
				if(age== "Custom") {
					$(this).next().toggle();
				}
			}
			
			return false;
		 });

	function AnimateVote(selector,newValue)
	{
		var curVal = 0;
		try{ curVal = parseInt(selector.text()); } catch(err){ curVal = 0;} 
		// Animate the element's value:
		if(isNaN(curVal)) curVal = 0;
		jQuery({value: curVal}).animate({value: newValue}, {
			duration: 1000,
			easing:'swing',
			step: function() {
				var newVal = Math.round(this.value*100)/100;
				selector.text(newVal);
			},
		});
	}
	function HateData()
	{
		$.modal.close();
		$(".nagmsg").hide();
		$(".standardmsg").show();
		$.cookie("suppressvote" + 12049,1);
	}
	function SubmitVote()
	{
		$("#submitvote").val("Voting...");
		setTimeout(function(){
			var beers = parseFloat($("#beervalue").text());
			var tech = parseFloat($("#techvalue").text());
			var accel = parseFloat($("#accelvalue").text());
			var elev = parseFloat($("#elevationvalue").text());
			var moist = parseFloat($("#moisturevalue").text());
			var raceID = 12049;
			
			$.post("procRaceRating.php", {raceID: raceID, beers: beers, tech: tech, accel:  accel,elev: elev, moisture: moist}, function( data, status, req) {
				
				$("#submitvote").val("Submit Vote");
				
				var response = eval(data);
				
				$.modal.close();
				
				AnimateVote($("#beerrating"),response[0].Beers);		
				
				$("#beerslider").attr("val",beers);
				
				AnimateVote($("#techrating"),response[0].Tech);
				$("#techslider").attr("val",tech);
				
				AnimateVote($("#accelrating"),response[0].Accel);
				$("#accelslider").attr("val",accel);
				
				AnimateVote($("#elevationrating"),response[0].Elev);
				$("#elevationslider").attr("val",elev);
				
				AnimateVote($("#moisturerating"),response[0].Moisture);
				$("#moistureslider").attr("val",moist);
				
				
			});
		},1000);
	}
    function ToggleVotes()
	{
		$("#votewindow").modal({overlayClose:true, maxHeight: 600, maxWidth: 700, width: 550});
		$(".slider").each(function() {
				var val = $(this).attr("val");
				$(this).parent().find(".ratingvalue").text(val);
				$(this).slider(
				{min: 1,
				max: 7,
				value: val,
				step: 0.1,
				slide: function(evt,ui) { UpdateSlider(ui,$(this)) },
				change: function(evt,ui) { UpdateSlider(ui,$(this)) }
				});
			});
	}
	function UpdateSlider(ui,jq)
	{
		jq.parent().find(".ratingvalue").text(ui.value);
	}
    function TogglePoints(raceCatID)
    {
		$(".points[RaceCatID=\'"+raceCatID+"\']").toggle();
    }
    
    var catsShown = false;
    function ToggleCats(raceCatID)
    {

		$(".placeInCat[RaceCatID=\'"+raceCatID+"\']").toggle();
        if(catsShown)
        {          
            $(".cat1").css({"border":'null'});
            $(".cat2").css({"border":'null'});
            $(".cat3").css({"border":'null'});
            $(".cat4").css({"border":'null'});
            $(".cat5").css({"border":'null'});
            $(".catX").css({"border":'null'});
        }
        else
        {
            $(".cat1").css({"border":'1px solid #FF0000'});
            $(".cat2").css({"border":'1px solid #FF6A00'});
            $(".cat3").css({"border":'1px solid #75FF56'});
            $(".cat4").css({"border":'1px solid #32D2FF'});
            $(".cat5").css({"border":'1px solid #000000'});
            $(".catX").css({"border":'1px solid #BBBBBB'});
        }
    }

<script type="text/javascript">
      var map = null;
      var setpin = false;
      var raceloc = null;
      var raceLL = null;
      var icon = "img/wheelicon.png";
      function GetMap(baseLL,stravaSegment)
      {        
        try{
			if(stravaSegment > 0 )
			{
                 var mapOptions = {
                        zoomControl: true,
                        zoomControlOptions: {
                            style: google.maps.ZoomControlStyle.SMALL
                            },
                        mapTypeControl: false,
                        streetViewControl: false,
                        zoom: 9,
                        mapTypeId: google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP
                    };
                    map = new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById("myMap"), mapOptions);
			
				    GetStravaPoints(stravaSegment);
			} 
            else 
            {
                 if(baseLL == null || baseLL.indexOf(":") == -1)
                 {
                    // todo hide map   
                    $("#rightracecolumn").hide();
                 }
                 else
                 {  
                    var s = baseLL.split(":");
                    //var ll = new google.maps.LatLng(s[0],s[1]);
            
                    //AddPushpin(ll);
                    var src =  "https://www.google.com/maps/embed/v1/place?key=AIzaSyD1jRF9AL8e8WPtZ04v3Ag9ua6nqFAivNU&zoom=9&q=" + s[0] + "," + s[1];
                    var iframe= '<iframe frameborder="0" style="border:0; width:100%; height: 100%" src="' + src + '" allowfullscreen></iframe>';
                
                    $("#myMap").html(iframe);
                }        
            }
            }
             catch(e)
             {
			    alert(e.message);
		    }
		if(baseLL == null || baseLL.indexOf(":") == -1 || !(stravaSegment > 0)) {
		         }
         
      }   
	  function GetStravaPoints(segmentId)
	  {
		$.get("strava.php?seg="+segmentId, function(data) {
				try{
					
					var points = decode(data.trim());
					

					 var poly = new google.maps.Polyline({
                      path: points,
                      geodesic: true,
                      strokeColor: '#FF7700',
                      strokeOpacity: 1.0,
                      strokeWeight: 2
                    });

                    poly.setMap(map);

                       var bounds = new google.maps.LatLngBounds();
                        poly.getPath().forEach(function(item, index) {
                            bounds.extend(new google.maps.LatLng(item.lat(), item.lng()));
                        });
                    map.fitBounds(bounds);
                    map.setOptions({mapTypeId: google.maps.MapTypeId.SATELLITE});
					$("#raceloc").text("Race Course");
					$("#stravainput").hide();
					$("#stravasegment").show();
					} catch(err) { alert(err.message);
					}
					
									
				});		
	  }
	  
	  function decode(encoded){

			// array that holds the points

			var points=[ ]
			var index = 0, len = encoded.length;
			var lat = 0, lng = 0;
			while (index < len) {
				var b, shift = 0, result = 0;
				do {

			b = encoded.charAt(index++).charCodeAt(0) - 63;//finds ascii                                                                                    //and substract it by 63
					  result |= (b & 0x1f) << shift;
					  shift += 5;
					 } while (b >= 0x20);


			   var dlat = ((result & 1) != 0 ? ~(result >> 1) : (result >> 1));
			   lat += dlat;
			  shift = 0;
			  result = 0;
			 do {
				b = encoded.charAt(index++).charCodeAt(0) - 63;
				result |= (b & 0x1f) << shift;
			   shift += 5;
				 } while (b >= 0x20);
			 var dlng = ((result & 1) != 0 ? ~(result >> 1) : (result >> 1));
			 lng += dlng;
 
		   points.push( new google.maps.LatLng(( lat / 1E5),( lng / 1E5)));  
 
		  }
		  return points
    }
	  
      function SetPinOnNextClick()
      {
        if(!setpin)
        {            
            document.getElementById("setpin").value = "Save";
        }
        else
        {
            var l = (raceLL.Latitude + ":" + raceLL.Longitude); 
            jQuery.get("procRaceLocation.php?raceID=12049&location="+l);
            document.getElementById("locationtools").innerHTML = "Thanks for the data!  Look for some cool maps soon.";
        }
        setpin = !setpin;
      }
      function FindLoc()
      {
         try
         {
            var search = document.getElementById("txtWhere").value;
            map.Find(null, search);
         }
         catch(e)
         {
            alert(e.message);
         }
      }
      function AddPushpin(latlong)
      {
        if(raceloc != null)
        {
            raceloc.setMap(null);
        }
        raceloc = new google.maps.Marker({
          position: latlong,
          map: map,
          icon: icon
        });   

        raceLL = latlong;          
        map.setCenter(latlong);
      }
      function MouseHandler(e)
      {
            if (e.leftMouseButton && setpin)
            {
                var ll;
                if(e.mapStyle != "o")
                {
                    // convert to latlong
                    var pixel = new VEPixel(e.mapX,e.mapY);
                    ll = map.PixelToLatLong(pixel);
                }
                else
                {
                    ll = e.latLong;
                }
                AddPushpin(ll);
            }
      }
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){ 
    $("#help").click(function(){ $("#helpdiv").toggle("slow") });
	
	
});
function VerifyUrl()
	{
		var url = $("#stravaurl").val();
		
		var legit = url && url.indexOf("strava.com/segments") >= 0;
		if(!legit)
		{
			alert("You need to submit a segment url.  You might be on a ride page -- on Strava, \"click go to segment page\" if you're looking at the segment in your own ride!");
		}
		return legit;
	}
</script>
